\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__logistic_8py_source_l00589}00589\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ n\_classes\ ==\ 2:}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__logistic_8py_source_l01668}01668\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ multi\_class\ :\ \{'auto,\ 'ovr',\ 'multinomial'\},\ default='auto'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__logistic_8py_source_l01669}01669\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ If\ the\ option\ chosen\ is\ 'ovr',\ then\ a\ binary\ problem\ is\ fit\ for\ each}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__logistic_8py_source_l01670}01670\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ label.\ For\ 'multinomial'\ the\ loss\ minimised\ is\ the\ multinomial\ loss\ fit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__logistic_8py_source_l01671}01671\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ across\ the\ entire\ probability\ distribution,\ *even\ when\ the\ data\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__logistic_8py_source_l01672}01672\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ binary*.\ 'multinomial'\ is\ unavailable\ when\ solver='liblinear'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__logistic_8py_source_l01673}01673\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 'auto'\ selects\ 'ovr'\ if\ the\ data\ is\ binary,\ or\ if\ solver='liblinear',}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__logistic_8py_source_l01674}01674\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ and\ otherwise\ selects\ 'multinomial'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__logistic_8py_source_l01675}01675\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__logistic_8py_source_l01676}01676\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ ..\ versionadded::\ 0.18}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__logistic_8py_source_l01677}01677\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Stochastic\ Average\ Gradient\ descent\ solver\ for\ 'multinomial'\ case.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__logistic_8py_source_l01678}01678\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ ..\ versionchanged::\ 0.22}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__logistic_8py_source_l01679}01679\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Default\ changed\ from\ 'ovr'\ to\ 'auto'\ in\ 0.22.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__logistic_8py_source_l01680}01680\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ ..\ deprecated::\ 1.5}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__logistic_8py_source_l01682}01682\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ From\ then\ on,\ the\ recommended\ 'multinomial'\ will\ always\ be\ used\ for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__logistic_8py_source_l01683}01683\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \`{}n\_classes\ >=\ 3\`{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__logistic_8py_source_l01684}01684\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Solvers\ that\ do\ not\ support\ 'multinomial'\ will\ raise\ an\ error.}}
